Serial sources cited in Notes field:
BL89 = British Library Document Supply Centre. 1989. Current serials received.
BS90 = BIOSIS. 1991. Serial sources for the BIOSIS Previews Database. Volume 1990.
BS94 = BIOSIS. 1994. Serial sources for the BIOSIS Previews Database. Volume 1994.
CAB90 = CAB. 1990. International Union List of Agricultural Serials.
CAS89 = Chemical Abstracts Service. 1990. CAS Source Index 1907-1989 Cumulative.
Melvyl = University of California online library catalog.
SPBM = BMNH. 1980. Serial Publications in the British Museum (Natural History) Library. 3rd ed.
UL = Titus (ed.) Union List of serials in libraries of the United States and Canada. 3rd edition.
WL(4) = Brown & Stratton (eds.) 1963-65. World List of Scientific Periodicals, 1900-1960. 4th ed.
ZRSS = BIOSIS. 1994. Zoological Record Serial Sources 1992/1994. 5th ed.
